TamperBench: Systematically Stress-Testing LLM Safety Under Fine-Tuning and Tampering
Authors: Saad Hossain, Tom Tseng, Punya Syon Pandey, Samanvay Vajpayee, Matthew Kowal, Nayeema Nonta, Samuel Simko, Stephen Casper, Zhijing Jin, Kellin Pelrine, Sirisha Rambhatla
First: 2026-02-06T18:04:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T23:27:30+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 15 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As increasingly capable open-weight large language models (LLMs) are deployed, improving their tamper resistance against unsafe modifications, whether accidental or intentional, becomes critical to minimize risks. However, there is no standard approach to evaluate tamper resistance. Varied datasets, metrics, and tampering configurations make it difficult to compare safety, utility, and robustness across different models and defenses. To address this, we introduce TamperBench, the first unified framework to systematically evaluate the tamper resistance of LLMs. TamperBench (i) curates a repository of state-of-the-art weight-space fine-tuning attacks, latent-space representation attacks, and alignment-stage defenses; (ii) enables realistic adversarial evaluation through systematic hyperparameter sweeps per attack-model pair; and (iii) provides both safety and utility evaluations. We use TamperBench to evaluate 21 open-weight LLMs, including defense-augmented variants, across nine tampering threats using standardized safety and capability metrics with hyperparameter sweeps per model-attack pair. The results provide insights including effects of post-training on tamper resistance, that jailbreak-tuning is typically the most severe attack, and that current alignment-stage defenses largely fail to withstand attack sweeps. Code is available at https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TamperBench：系统性压力测试LLM在微调和篡改下的安全性
随着越来越强大的开放权重大型语言模型（LLM）的部署，提高其对不安全修改的篡改抵抗能力，无论是意外还是故意的，变得至关重要，以最小化风险。然而，目前没有标准的方法来评估篡改抵抗力。不同的数据集、指标和篡改配置使得比较不同模型和防御的安全性、实用性和鲁棒性变得困难。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了TamperBench，这是第一个统一框架，用于系统性评估LLM的篡改抵抗力。TamperBench (i) 收集了最先进的权重空间微调攻击、潜在空间表示攻击和对齐阶段防御的库；(ii) 通过对每个攻击-模型对进行系统的超参数搜索，实现现实的对抗性评估；(iii) 提供安全性和实用性评估。我们使用TamperBench评估了21个开放权重LLM，包括增强防御的变体，针对九种篡改威胁使用标准化的安全性和能力指标，并对每个模型-攻击对进行超参数搜索。结果提供了包括后训练对篡改抵抗力影响的见解，越狱微调通常是最严重的攻击，以及当前对齐阶段的防御在很大程度上未能抵御攻击的结果。代码可在https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for improving the tamper resistance of large language models (LLMs) against unsafe modifications, as existing evaluation methods lack standardization and comparability due to diverse datasets and metrics. Previous approaches have not systematically assessed the safety and robustness of LLMs under various tampering scenarios, leading to inconsistent results. The proposed framework, TamperBench, offers a unified method to evaluate tamper resistance by curating a repository of attacks and defenses, enabling systematic hyperparameter sweeps, and providing comprehensive safety and utility evaluations. This paper contributes by systematically evaluating 21 open-weight LLMs against nine tampering threats, revealing insights such as the severe impact of jailbreak-tuning and the inadequacy of current defenses. The methodology demonstrates that TamperBench can effectively assess the tamper resistance of LLMs, supporting the goal of enhancing their safety and robustness.
本研究解决了提高大型语言模型（LLM）对不安全修改的抗篡改能力的迫切需求，因为现有的评估方法缺乏标准化和可比性。以往的方法依赖于不同的数据集和指标，导致在不同模型之间评估安全性和鲁棒性时遇到困难。提出的TamperBench框架提供了一种统一的方法，通过整理攻击和防御的库，能够进行现实的对抗性评估，并提供全面的安全性和效用评估，从而系统地评估LLM的抗篡改能力。本文的贡献在于对21个开放权重的LLM在九种篡改威胁下进行评估，揭示了后训练效果对抗篡改能力的显著影响，以及当前防御措施通常不足的情况。该方法包括对每个模型-攻击对进行超参数搜索，产生标准化的性能指标，以支持框架增强LLM安全性的目标。
When Autoregressive Consistency Hurts Safety Alignment
Authors: Bochen Lyu, Yiyang Jia, Xiaohao Cai, Zhanxing Zhu
First: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00
Comments: 21 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment in large language models (LLMs) is fragile in part because it is often shallow: fine-tuning mainly reshapes the model's behavior near the first few output tokens. We argue that this phenomenon can be understood through autoregressive consistency, the tendency of next-token prediction to preserve and extend the current response trajectory consistently. By analyzing the learning dynamics of safety alignment, we show that autoregressive consistency can concentrate alignment updates on early tokens, offering a mechanistic explanation for shallow safety alignment. The same mechanism also predicts a broader class of attacks on LLMs: attacks that induce harmful continuation states at arbitrary positions in the output trajectory. As a concrete example, we introduce random insertion attack, which inserts a short harmful span into an otherwise safe refusal trajectory and exploits autoregressive consistency to sustain the resulting harmful branch, thereby bypassing safety alignment. Notably, a short harmful span can redirect the generation to be harmful even after a long refusal prefix, highlighting autoregressive consistency as a potential broader failure mechanism. This suggests that safety alignment should also break harmful autoregressive consistency throughout the output trajectory. We therefore propose adversarial safety alignment, an initial framework based on worst-case harmful continuation states, and instantiate it with random worst-insertion training. Overall, our results suggest that autoregressive consistency should be treated as a central consideration in both safety alignment and attack design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归一致性如何损害安全对齐
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐脆弱，部分原因在于其通常较浅：微调主要重塑模型在前几个输出标记附近的行为。我们认为，这一现象可以通过自回归一致性来理解，即下一个标记预测保持并延续当前响应轨迹的一致性倾向。通过分析安全对齐的学习动态，我们表明自回归一致性可以将对齐更新集中在早期标记上，为浅层安全对齐提供了机制性解释。同样的机制也预测了一类更广泛的对LLMs的攻击：在输出轨迹的任意位置诱导有害延续状态的攻击。作为具体例子，我们引入随机插入攻击，该攻击将一个短的有害片段插入到原本安全的拒绝轨迹中，并利用自回归一致性来维持由此产生的有害分支，从而绕过安全对齐。值得注意的是，一个短的有害片段可以在长拒绝前缀后重新引导生成变得有害，突显自回归一致性作为潜在的更广泛失败机制。这表明安全对齐也应打破输出轨迹中有害的自回归一致性。因此，我们提出了对抗性安全对齐，这是一个基于最坏情况有害延续状态的初步框架，并通过随机最坏插入训练进行实例化。总体而言，我们的结果表明，自回归一致性应被视为安全对齐和攻击设计中的核心考虑。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the fragility of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which is often superficial due to fine-tuning primarily affecting the initial output tokens. Previous methods have focused on aligning model behavior without adequately addressing the tendency of autoregressive consistency to reinforce early token predictions, leading to shallow safety alignment. The proposed approach, adversarial safety alignment, aims to counteract this issue by considering harmful continuation states throughout the output trajectory, thus providing a more robust framework for safety alignment. The methodology includes random worst-insertion training to mitigate the risks posed by autoregressive consistency, which can facilitate harmful outputs even after safe refusals. The findings indicate that this new approach significantly enhances safety alignment by addressing the limitations of existing methods, thereby supporting the goal of creating safer LLMs.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全对齐的脆弱性，这种脆弱性通常仅限于初始输出标记，原因在于自回归一致性。以往的方法主要集中于微调，导致安全对齐较为浅显，未能考虑有害的延续状态。提出的方法，即对抗性安全对齐，旨在通过考虑最坏情况下的有害延续状态并采用随机最坏插入训练来缓解这些问题。这一方法揭示了自回归一致性可能导致显著的脆弱性，具体体现在引入了一种随机插入攻击，该攻击利用这种一致性绕过安全措施。研究结果表明，解决自回归一致性问题对于增强安全对齐和开发强健的防御机制至关重要，从而为理解LLM的脆弱性和安全机制做出了贡献。
Black-box, Adaptive, Efficient, Transferable, Harmful, Applicable... Attacks Are All You Need to Break LLMs
Authors: Vincent Limbach, Jonas Dornbusch, David Lüdke, Stephan Günnemann, Leo Schwinn
First: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurately evaluating adversarial robustness is a longstanding challenge. A flawed attack design can inflate robustness estimates, making deployment risk assessment and defense comparison unreliable. Historically, standardized attacks such as AutoAttack have largely resolved this for image classifiers, providing a reliable evaluation baseline for systematic comparison across defenses. However, no equivalent exists for LLM jailbreak evaluation yet, where designing such an attack is considerably more difficult. A reliable attack must, among other things, be black-box compatible, applicable to arbitrary defense pipelines, and efficient, which no existing method jointly satisfies. We introduce Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), a masked diffusion language model attacker trained via iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, requiring only black-box access to the target. The same method can be used without modification as a strong adaptive attack on individual behaviors, or as an efficient amortized policy that transfers to held-out behaviors and unseen target models without fine-tuning. Even against layered defenses, such as a Circuit Breaker-trained model combined with an auxiliary detector, IHO improves attack success considerably over state-of-the-art approaches, without any defense-specific adaptation. Our results position IHO as a practical step toward the kind of standardized jailbreak evaluation that has improved reliability in the past. Code and models are available on GitHub and Hugging Face.
中文标题/摘要
标题：黑箱、自适应、高效、可转移、有害、适用……攻击是破解LLM所需的一切
准确评估对抗鲁棒性一直是一个长期挑战。设计不当的攻击可能会夸大鲁棒性估计，使得部署风险评估和防御比较不可靠。历史上，标准化攻击如AutoAttack在图像分类器中基本解决了这一问题，为系统比较提供了可靠的评估基准。然而，目前尚无等效的LLM越狱评估标准，设计这样的攻击要困难得多。一个可靠的攻击必须在其他条件下兼容黑箱，适用于任意防御管道，并且高效，而现有方法没有一个能同时满足这些条件。我们引入了间接有害优化（IHO），这是一种通过迭代偏好优化训练的掩蔽扩散语言模型攻击者，针对有害性评估者，仅需黑箱访问目标。相同的方法可以在不修改的情况下作为对个体行为的强自适应攻击，或作为一种高效的摊销策略，能够转移到未见的目标模型和保留行为，而无需微调。即使面对分层防御，如与辅助检测器结合的电路断路器训练模型，IHO在攻击成功率上显著超越了最先进的方法，而无需任何特定于防御的适应。我们的结果将IHO定位为朝着标准化越狱评估的实用步骤，这在过去提高了可靠性。代码和模型可在GitHub和Hugging Face上获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of accurately evaluating adversarial robustness in large language models (LLMs), highlighting that existing methods, such as standardized attacks for image classifiers, do not adequately apply to LLM jailbreak evaluations. Previous approaches often fail to meet the necessary criteria of being black-box compatible, applicable to various defense mechanisms, and efficient, leading to unreliable robustness estimates. The proposed method, Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), is a masked diffusion language model attacker that utilizes iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, allowing for effective black-box attacks without the need for defense-specific adaptations. This methodology not only serves as a robust adaptive attack on individual behaviors but also efficiently transfers to new behaviors and unseen models. The experimental results demonstrate that IHO significantly enhances attack success rates against layered defenses compared to state-of-the-art methods, thereby contributing to the establishment of a standardized evaluation framework for LLM jailbreaks.
本研究解决了准确评估大型语言模型（LLMs）对抗鲁棒性的问题，强调了现有攻击设计的不足，这些设计会夸大鲁棒性估计，妨碍可靠的风险评估。过去的方法，如针对图像分类器的标准化攻击，无法有效转化为LLMs，因为设计黑箱兼容且适用于各种防御机制的攻击相当复杂。提出的间接危害优化（IHO）方法通过利用仅需黑箱访问的掩蔽扩散语言模型攻击者克服了这些局限性，使其既可以作为对特定行为的自适应攻击，也可以作为高效的策略，能够在不进行微调的情况下转移到新模型。论文表明，IHO显著提高了对先进防御的攻击成功率，使其成为建立LLM越狱标准化评估方法的可行方案，从而为该领域提供了更可靠的评估。
D-Judge: Disrupting Multi-Turn Jailbreaks using Semantics-Preserving Output Rewriting
Authors: Huanli Gong, Zhipeng Wei, Yu Fu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Ananya Gupta, Yue Dong, N. Benjamin Erichson
First: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00
Comments: Proceedings of the 43rd International Conference on Machine Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn jailbreak attacks pose a growing threat to large language model (LLM) safety because they exploit feedback from auxiliary judge models to iteratively refine prompts toward harmful goals. Existing defenses largely detect or block unsafe content at individual turns or at the final response, leaving the judge-driven refinement loop intact and allowing attackers to extract informative feedback from intermediate interactions. We introduce D-Judge, a semantics-preserving output rewriting defense that intervenes directly in this loop by rewriting the victim LLM's responses before they are evaluated by the attacker's judge. By misaligning the judge's feedback signal without changing the meaning of the original response, D-Judge derails the attacker's prompt-refinement process, causing subsequent queries to be optimized against a distorted signal of attack progress. To improve D-Judge's ability to produce such rewrites, we construct a dataset of semantically equivalent response pairs that induce different judge-assigned harmfulness scores, and use it for supervised fine-tuning followed by direct preference optimization. Experiments on HarmBench show that D-Judge reduces the success rate of state-of-the-art multi-turn jailbreaks while preserving performance on benign benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：D-Judge：通过语义保持输出重写来破坏多轮越狱攻击
多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLM）安全构成日益严重的威胁，因为它们利用辅助评判模型的反馈，迭代地优化提示以达到有害目标。现有防御主要在单个回合或最终响应中检测或阻止不安全内容，保持评判驱动的优化循环不变，使攻击者能够从中间交互中提取有用反馈。我们提出了D-Judge，一种语义保持输出重写防御，直接干预这一循环，通过在攻击者的评判之前重写受害者LLM的响应。通过在不改变原始响应含义的情况下使评判的反馈信号失真，D-Judge使攻击者的提示优化过程偏离轨道，导致后续查询针对扭曲的攻击进展信号进行优化。为了提高D-Judge生成此类重写的能力，我们构建了一个语义等价响应对的数据集，该数据集引发不同的评判分配有害性评分，并用于监督微调，随后进行直接偏好优化。在HarmBench上的实验表明，D-Judge在保持良性基准性能的同时，降低了最先进的多轮越狱攻击的成功率。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the increasing threat posed by multi-turn jailbreak attacks on large language models (LLMs), which exploit feedback from auxiliary judge models to refine harmful prompts. Previous methods primarily focused on detecting or blocking unsafe content at individual turns or final responses, failing to disrupt the iterative feedback loop that attackers utilize. The proposed D-Judge approach differs by rewriting the LLM's outputs before they are assessed by the judge, thereby misaligning the feedback signal while maintaining the original response's meaning. This method effectively disrupts the prompt-refinement process of attackers. The paper contributes a novel defense mechanism that utilizes a dataset of semantically equivalent response pairs to enhance the rewriting process through supervised fine-tuning and preference optimization. Experimental results on HarmBench demonstrate that D-Judge significantly reduces the success rate of advanced multi-turn jailbreaks while maintaining performance on benign tasks.
本研究针对多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLMs）日益增长的威胁，这些攻击利用辅助评估模型的反馈来逐步完善有害提示。以往的方法主要集中在检测或阻止单个回合或最终响应中的不安全内容，未能打断攻击者利用的迭代反馈循环。提出的D-Judge方法通过直接干预这一循环而有所不同，重写LLM的响应，以在不改变原意的情况下使评估者的反馈失去一致性，从而破坏攻击者的完善过程。这种方法的动机明确，因为它针对攻击的核心机制。本文贡献了一组语义等价的响应对的数据集，用于对D-Judge进行微调，实验表明该方法在HarmBench数据集上显著降低了先进多轮越狱攻击的成功率，同时在良性任务上保持了性能。
Quality-Diversity Evolution for Discovering Diverse Vulnerabilities in LLM Safety
Authors: Subhadip Mitra
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-05-30T16:40:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T16:40:24+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 6 figures. Accepted at the ICLR 2026 Workshop on Agents in the Wild (AIWILD)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Current approaches to LLM adversarial testing suffer from coverage gaps: manual red-teaming does not scale, LLM-as-attacker methods exhibit mode collapse, and gradient-based approaches produce uninterpretable gibberish. We introduce a quality-diversity evolutionary framework that operates at the semantic level, evolving interpretable attack strategies rather than token sequences. Using MAP-Elites, we maintain a diverse archive of attacks across behavioral dimensions (strategy type, encoding method, prompt length). In experiments across GPT-4o-mini, Claude 3.5 Sonnet, Gemini 2.0 Flash, and an open-weight coding model (Devstral-small-2), we discover distinct vulnerability profiles: GPT-4o-mini is vulnerable to hypothetical and multi-turn framing combined with ROT13 encoding (fitness 0.8), Gemini to direct attacks with ROT13 and multi-turn with Leetspeak (0.8), while Claude shows uniformly ambiguous responses across all strategies (max 0.4). The semantic representation produces interpretable attacks that reveal systematic, model-specific weaknesses, providing actionable insights for improving LLM safety and a reproducible baseline for evaluating future frontier models. Code and experiment artifacts are released at https://github.com/bassrehab/red-queen.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于发现LLM安全性中多样化脆弱性的质量-多样性进化
当前LLM对抗测试的方法存在覆盖缺口：手动红队无法扩展，LLM作为攻击者的方法表现出模式崩溃，基于梯度的方法产生不可解释的乱码。我们引入了一种在语义层面上操作的质量-多样性进化框架，进化可解释的攻击策略而非令牌序列。使用MAP-Elites，我们维护一个跨行为维度（策略类型、编码方法、提示长度）的多样化攻击档案。在对GPT-4o-mini、Claude 3.5 Sonnet、Gemini 2.0 Flash和一个开放权重编码模型（Devstral-small-2）的实验中，我们发现了不同的脆弱性特征：GPT-4o-mini对假设性和多轮框架结合ROT13编码（适应度0.8）脆弱，Gemini对直接攻击使用ROT13和多轮使用Leetspeak（0.8）脆弱，而Claude在所有策略中表现出均匀模糊的响应（最大0.4）。语义表示产生可解释的攻击，揭示系统性、模型特定的弱点，为改善LLM安全性提供可操作的见解，并为评估未来前沿模型提供可重复的基线。代码和实验文物已发布在https://github.com/bassrehab/red-queen。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of current methods in adversarial testing of large language models (LLMs), which include manual red-teaming that lacks scalability, LLM-as-attacker methods prone to mode collapse, and gradient-based approaches yielding unintelligible outputs. The proposed quality-diversity evolutionary framework overcomes these issues by evolving interpretable attack strategies at the semantic level rather than focusing solely on token sequences, thus maintaining a diverse archive of attacks based on various behavioral dimensions. This paper contributes to the field by revealing distinct vulnerability profiles for different LLMs, such as GPT-4o-mini and Gemini 2.0, through experiments that demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method in identifying model-specific weaknesses with interpretable attacks. The methodology employs MAP-Elites to systematically explore and document these vulnerabilities, achieving notable fitness scores and providing a reproducible baseline for future evaluations of LLM safety.
本研究解决了当前大型语言模型（LLM）对抗测试方法的局限性，包括缺乏可扩展性的人工红队、遭遇模式崩溃的LLM作为攻击者的方法，以及产生难以理解输出的基于梯度的技术。所提出的质量-多样性进化框架通过在语义层面上进化可解释的攻击策略，而不仅仅是生成标记序列，从而克服了这些问题。该论文的贡献在于使用MAP-Elites维护一个跨各种行为维度的多样化攻击档案，从而发现GPT-4o-mini、Gemini 2.0 Flash和Claude 3.5 Sonnet等模型的特定脆弱性。该方法论涉及对这些模型进行系统实验，揭示了特定的弱点，例如GPT-4o-mini对某些编码方法和提示策略的脆弱性，性能指标表明为改善LLM安全性提供了可操作的见解，并为未来评估建立了可重复的基线。
The Refusal--Compliance Tradeoff: A Large-Scale Safety Behavior Audit of Large Language Models
Authors: Alif Al Hasan, Sumon Biswas
First: 2026-05-06T20:35:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T15:07:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Refusal rates are a poor proxy for LLM safety, i.e., a model may over-refuse benign prompts while still complying with harmful ones. We audit both failure modes across 21 open-weight LLMs on four safety benchmarks (OR-Bench, XSTest, ToxiGen, BOLD), using a composition adjustment to isolate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity confounds. We report three findings. First, models adopt fundamentally different calibration strategies: conservative ecosystems such as Llama suppress unsafe outputs at the cost of elevated over-refusals, while permissive ecosystems such as DeepSeek and Qwen preserve helpfulness but tolerate higher harmful compliance. Second, demographic protection is unequal: models over-protect prominent racial and religious groups, frequently refusing even benign prompts about them, while providing substantially weaker protection against disability-targeted attacks. Third, refusal and compliance tendencies are stable within model families across generations and scales, suggesting that post-training objectives shape safety behavior more than architecture. Our results call for joint, demographically-aware, and multi-judge safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：拒绝与合规权衡：大规模语言模型的安全行为审计
拒绝率是大型语言模型安全性的不良代理，即模型可能在过度拒绝良性提示的同时仍然对有害提示做出反应。我们在四个安全基准（OR-Bench、XSTest、ToxiGen、BOLD）上审计了21个开放权重的LLM，使用组合调整来隔离模型敏感性与数据集毒性混淆。我们报告了三个发现。首先，模型采用根本不同的校准策略：保守生态系统如Llama在提高过度拒绝的代价下抑制不安全输出，而宽松生态系统如DeepSeek和Qwen则保持有用性但容忍更高的有害合规。其次，人口保护不平等：模型过度保护显著的种族和宗教群体，频繁拒绝关于它们的良性提示，而对残疾目标攻击提供的保护则明显较弱。第三，拒绝和合规倾向在模型家族中跨代和规模保持稳定，表明后训练目标在塑造安全行为方面的影响大于架构。我们的结果呼吁进行联合、关注人口统计和多评审的安全评估。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the inadequacy of refusal rates as indicators of safety in large language models (LLMs), highlighting that models may refuse benign prompts while complying with harmful ones. Previous methods primarily focused on refusal rates without considering the nuances of model behavior, leading to misleading assessments of safety. The proposed approach involves auditing 21 open-weight LLMs across four safety benchmarks while adjusting for dataset toxicity, allowing for a clearer understanding of model sensitivity. The study contributes by revealing distinct calibration strategies among models, demonstrating unequal demographic protections, and indicating that safety behavior is more influenced by post-training objectives than by architecture. The methodology effectively assesses safety behavior, showing that models exhibit stable refusal and compliance tendencies, which supports the need for more comprehensive and demographically aware safety evaluations.
本研究探讨了拒绝率作为大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性指标的不足，强调模型可能拒绝良性提示而接受有害内容。以往的方法主要集中在测量拒绝率，而未考虑模型行为的细微差别，导致安全性评估误导。提出的方法对21个开放权重的LLMs进行了全面审计，涵盖四个安全基准，利用组合调整来区分模型敏感性与数据集毒性。研究发现，模型表现出不同的校准策略，保守模型如Llama优先考虑安全性，但增加了拒绝率，而宽松模型如DeepSeek则保持有用性，但允许更高的有害合规性。此外，研究揭示了保护水平的种族差异，模型对某些群体的保护过度，而对其他群体的保护不足。研究结果表明，安全行为更多地受到后训练目标的影响，而非模型架构，倡导采用更细致、关注人口统计的安全评估框架。
How Reliable Are AI Attackers Against a Fixed Vulnerable Target? A 400-Run Empirical Study of LLM Penetration Testing Consistency
Authors: Galip Tolga Erdem
First: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00
Comments: 41 pages, 7 figures. Code and 400-run dataset: https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20421592
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) can autonomously conduct multi-stage cyber attacks, but the consistency of their offensive behavior under repeated trials remains unstudied. This work presents the first large-scale empirical measurement of LLM attack consistency: 400 autonomous penetration testing runs (4 models, 100 each) against an identical honeypot hosting OWASP Juice Shop and two additional vulnerable services, holding prompt, orchestrator, and target constant. No model emitted a content refusal that survived the orchestrator's one-shot authorization re-prompt at iterations 0-1. Claude Sonnet 4's API calls did encounter upstream service unavailability - 91 of 1,135 calls returned HTTP 529 overloaded_error during a documented Anthropic capacity event, truncating 39 of 100 Claude runs. An earlier draft catalogued these as safety refusals; on full-log audit they are upstream API failures, not model-level refusals. Despite this, Claude achieved full exploitation in 61 of 100 runs; Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite in 85; GPT-4o-mini in 56 while deploying 98 unique attack strategies; qwen2.5-coder:14b in 25. Failure modes are model-distinctive: Claude through API truncation (39 runs), qwen through premature completion (52), GPT-4o-mini through iteration-budget exhaustion (23). Cross-service credential reuse appeared only in configurations retaining the most conversation history (qwen 57%, GPT-4o-mini 49%, cloud models 0% on 5-exchange windows). Cross-model exploitation rate differences are statistically significant (p < 0.001) with large effect sizes; qwen vs. Gemini SQL injection rates differ at Cohen's h = 1.12. First-exploit timing fell within a 15-30 second wall-clock range. To our knowledge, this is the first study to measure autonomous LLM attack behavior at N=100 per model across a multi-service target.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI攻击者对固定脆弱目标的可靠性如何？一项400次运行的LLM渗透测试一致性实证研究
大型语言模型（LLMs）可以自主进行多阶段网络攻击，但其在重复试验中的攻击行为一致性尚未研究。本研究首次大规模实证测量LLM攻击一致性：对一个托管OWASP Juice Shop和两个额外脆弱服务的相同蜜罐进行400次自主渗透测试（4个模型，各100次），保持提示、协调者和目标不变。在迭代0-1中，没有模型发出经过协调者一次性授权重新提示后仍然有效的内容拒绝。Claude Sonnet 4的API调用确实遇到了上游服务不可用的情况——在一次记录的Anthropic容量事件中，1,135次调用中有91次返回HTTP 529 overloaded_error，截断了100次Claude运行中的39次。早期草稿将这些列为安全拒绝；经过完整日志审计后，它们被认定为上游API故障，而非模型级拒绝。尽管如此，Claude在100次运行中实现了61次完全利用；Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite为85次；GPT-4o-mini为56次，同时部署了98种独特的攻击策略；qwen2.5-coder:14b为25次。失败模式具有模型特征：Claude通过API截断（39次运行），qwen通过过早完成（52次），GPT-4o-mini通过迭代预算耗尽（23次）。跨服务凭证重用仅出现在保留最多对话历史的配置中（qwen 57%，GPT-4o-mini 49%，云模型在5次交换窗口中为0%）。跨模型利用率差异具有统计显著性（p < 0.001），效应量大；qwen与Gemini的SQL注入率差异为Cohen's h = 1.12。首次利用的时间落在15-30秒的实际时间范围内。据我们所知，这是首个测量自主LLM攻击行为的研究，N=100每个模型，跨多个服务目标。
Summary / 总结
This research investigates the consistency of large language models (LLMs) in conducting autonomous multi-stage cyber attacks, an area that has not been previously studied. Past methods lacked empirical measurement of attack consistency, leading to misconceptions about model behavior during penetration testing. The contribution of the paper lies in its systematic measurement of attack behavior, revealing significant differences in exploitation rates and failure modes among models. The methodology employed includes controlled trials with constant prompts and orchestrators, resulting in varied performance: Claude achieved full exploitation in 61% of runs, Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite in 85%, and GPT-4o-mini in 56%, demonstrating statistically significant differences in attack strategies and success rates, thus supporting the research goals.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在自主网络攻击中表现出的攻击行为一致性，这是一个之前未被研究的领域。以往的方法缺乏对攻击一致性的实证测量，导致对LLMs在渗透测试中可靠性的疑虑。所提出的方法涉及在固定的蜜罐上对四种不同模型进行400次自主渗透测试，保持试验条件不变。本研究通过提供对每个模型性能和失败模式的详细见解，为理解LLM攻击行为做出了贡献，揭示了利用率和策略之间的显著差异。研究结果表明，尽管Claude和Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite等模型达到了较高的利用率，但不同模型之间的性能差异显著，观察到的差异具有统计显著性，从而支持了评估LLM在网络攻击场景中可靠性的目标。
Beyond Attack Success Rate: Temporal Logit Observability for LLM Safety Failures
Authors: Junyoung Park, Sunghwan Park, Seongyong Ju, Jaewoo Lee
First: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Attack Success Rate (ASR) evaluates each jailbreak with a single yes/no label at the end of generation, telling us whether a failure happened but not how it unfolded. Two attacks that produce equally harmful outputs may have followed completely different paths, and ASR cannot tell them apart. We make those hidden paths observable from logits alone. Temporal Logit Observability (TLO) is a training-free diagnostic that watches a compliance-refusal margin during decoding and places each model-attack condition on a calibrated 2D plane. By design, this plane is most informative exactly where ASR is least informative: among attacks that succeed for genuinely different reasons. Across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, attacks with nearly identical ASR land at clearly different points on the plane: the same model can fail through different temporal patterns. The geometry matches refusal-direction probes from hidden states on most conditions, with one model showing the limit of our fixed-lexicon approach. A simple early-stop rule derived from TLO cuts successful jailbreaks by more than half, without false alarms on plain benign queries. Safety evaluation should report when and how a failure unfolds, not only whether it occurred. TLO makes the first two observable from logits alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越攻击成功率：LLM安全失败的时间逻辑可观测性
攻击成功率（ASR）在生成结束时用单一的是/否标签评估每个越狱，告诉我们是否发生了失败，但不说明其过程。两个产生同样有害输出的攻击可能遵循完全不同的路径，而ASR无法区分它们。我们使这些隐藏路径仅通过逻辑可观测。时间逻辑可观测性（TLO）是一种无训练的诊断方法，在解码过程中观察合规-拒绝边际，并将每个模型-攻击条件放置在一个校准的二维平面上。根据设计，这个平面在ASR信息最少的地方最具信息性：在因真正不同原因而成功的攻击之间。在四个对齐的LLM和三种越狱范式中，几乎相同的ASR攻击在平面上位于明显不同的点：同一模型可以通过不同的时间模式失败。几何形状与大多数条件下隐藏状态的拒绝方向探测相匹配，其中一个模型显示了我们固定词汇表方法的极限。基于TLO的简单早停规则将成功的越狱减少了一半以上，而在普通良性查询上没有误报。安全评估应报告失败何时以及如何展开，而不仅仅是是否发生。TLO使前两者仅通过逻辑可观测。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the limitations of the Attack Success Rate (ASR) metric, which only indicates whether a jailbreak attack on large language models (LLMs) was successful without providing insights into the underlying processes. Previous methods have relied on ASR, which fails to differentiate between attacks that yield similar harmful outputs but follow distinct paths. The proposed approach, Temporal Logit Observability (TLO), offers a training-free diagnostic that visualizes compliance-refusal margins during decoding, allowing for a more nuanced understanding of attack dynamics. The contribution of this paper lies in its ability to reveal the hidden paths of attacks through a calibrated 2D plane, demonstrating that attacks with identical ASR can originate from different temporal patterns. The methodology was tested across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, achieving a significant reduction in successful jailbreaks by over 50% with no false alarms on benign queries, thereby supporting the goal of enhancing safety evaluations by detailing how failures occur rather than merely confirming their existence.

Aligned but Fragile: Enhancing LLM Safety Robustness via Zeroth-Order Optimization
Authors: Zhihao Liu, Yifan Wu, Jian Lou, Di Wang, Yuxi Zhou, Yuke Hu
First: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment for large language models (LLMs) aims to reduce harmful or unsafe behavior while preserving general utility. However, recent findings reveal that alignment effects can be fragile: lightweight post-alignment manipulations, such as parameter noise, activation noise, or quantization, can easily weaken the intended safety behavior. Prior efforts to improve robustness have primarily focused on data curation, modified alignment objectives, and safety-critical parameter identification, leaving the role of the optimizer itself largely unexplored. In this paper, we are the first to study the robustness of safety alignment from the perspective of the base optimizer. This optimizer-centric view naturally points to zeroth-order optimization, which provides a robustness-oriented signal by evaluating safety alignment under perturbations. Based on this insight, we propose a hybrid framework that first performs standard first-order safety alignment and then applies zeroth-order refinement to improve robustness. Both theoretically and empirically, we show that only a few zeroth-order refinement steps can enhance robustness while preserving safety alignment. We further improve the efficiency of zeroth-order refinement by exploiting its inherent perturbation-based evaluations to estimate layer-wise robustness sensitivity, enabling the refinement process to concentrate updates on robustness-critical layers with modest training overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐但脆弱：通过零阶优化增强大型语言模型的安全性鲁棒性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐旨在减少有害或不安全行为，同时保持一般效用。然而，最近的研究发现，对齐效果可能是脆弱的：轻量级的后对齐操作，如参数噪声、激活噪声或量化，可能会轻易削弱预期的安全行为。以往提高鲁棒性的努力主要集中在数据策划、修改对齐目标和安全关键参数识别上，而优化器本身的作用则大多未被探索。 在本文中，我们首次从基础优化器的角度研究安全对齐的鲁棒性。这种以优化器为中心的视角自然指向零阶优化，它通过在扰动下评估安全对齐提供了一个面向鲁棒性的信号。基于这一见解，我们提出了一个混合框架，首先执行标准的一阶安全对齐，然后应用零阶精炼以提高鲁棒性。我们在理论和实证上都表明，仅需少量的零阶精炼步骤即可在保持安全对齐的同时增强鲁棒性。我们进一步通过利用零阶精炼固有的基于扰动的评估来估计层级鲁棒性敏感性，提高了零阶精炼的效率，使精炼过程能够将更新集中在鲁棒性关键层上，且训练开销适中。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the fragility of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), where lightweight manipulations can undermine intended safety behaviors. Previous methods have focused on data curation and modified alignment objectives, but they have largely neglected the role of the optimizer, which this paper seeks to explore. The authors propose a novel hybrid framework that combines standard first-order safety alignment with zeroth-order optimization to enhance robustness without sacrificing safety. This approach is well-motivated as it leverages the optimizer's capabilities to evaluate safety alignment under perturbations. The methodology demonstrates that a few steps of zeroth-order refinement can significantly improve robustness while maintaining safety alignment, achieving efficient updates focused on critical layers with minimal training overhead.
本研究解决了大型语言模型（LLMs）中的安全对齐挑战，旨在最小化有害行为，同时保持实用性。以往的方法主要集中在数据整理和修改对齐目标上，但往往忽视了优化器的作用，导致脆弱的对齐效果容易受到小扰动的影响。本文提出了一种以零阶优化为中心的新方法，该方法在扰动下评估安全对齐，以增强鲁棒性。该方法论包括一个混合框架，结合了标准的一阶安全对齐和零阶精炼，证明了少量的精炼步骤可以显著提高鲁棒性而不影响安全对齐。实验结果表明，该方法有效增强了鲁棒性，同时保持了安全性，支持了创建更具韧性的LLMs的目标。
SelfGrader: LLM Jailbreak Detection via Anchored Token-Level Logits
Authors: Zikai Zhang, Rui Hu, Olivera Kotevska, Jiahao Xu
First: 2026-04-01T23:29:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:44:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are powerful tools for answering user queries, yet they remain highly vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing guardrail methods typically rely on internal features or textual responses to detect malicious queries, which either introduce substantial latency or suffer from randomness in text generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose SelfGrader, a lightweight guardrail method that formulates jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits. Specifically, SelfGrader evaluates the safety of a user query within a compact set of numerical tokens (NTs) (e.g., 0-9) and interprets their logit distribution as an internal safety signal. To align these signals with the target safety rubric, SelfGrader constructs Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and introduces a dual-perspective scoring rule that considers both the maliciousness and benignness of the query, yielding a stable and interpretable score that reflects harmfulness and reduces the false positive rate simultaneously. Extensive experiments across diverse jailbreak benchmarks, adaptive attacks, benign prompt benchmarks, multiple LLMs, and state-of-the-art guardrail baselines demonstrate that SelfGrader achieves strong robustness with low false positive rates, memory overhead, and latency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SelfGrader：通过锚定的令牌级逻辑进行LLM越狱检测
大型语言模型（LLMs）是回答用户查询的强大工具，但它们仍然高度易受越狱攻击。现有的防护方法通常依赖于内部特征或文本响应来检测恶意查询，这要么引入了显著的延迟，要么在文本生成中遭受随机性。为克服这些限制，我们提出了SelfGrader，这是一种轻量级的防护方法，将越狱检测公式化为使用锚定令牌级逻辑的数值评分问题。具体而言，SelfGrader在一组紧凑的数值令牌（NTs）（例如，0-9）中评估用户查询的安全性，并将其逻辑分布解释为内部安全信号。为了将这些信号与目标安全标准对齐，SelfGrader构建了可能近似正确指导的ICL锚定示例，并引入了一种双视角评分规则，考虑查询的恶意性和良性，从而产生一个稳定且可解释的分数，反映有害性并同时降低误报率。在多种越狱基准、适应性攻击、良性提示基准、多个LLM和最先进的防护基线上的广泛实验表明，SelfGrader在低误报率、内存开销和延迟方面实现了强大的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the vulnerability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks, which existing guardrail methods struggle to effectively mitigate due to their reliance on internal features or textual responses that can introduce latency and randomness. The proposed approach, SelfGrader, differs by framing jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits, which allows for a more stable and interpretable evaluation of user queries. This method is well-motivated as it aims to reduce false positives while maintaining robustness against various attack types. SelfGrader employs Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and a dual-perspective scoring rule to assess both malicious and benign queries. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks indicate that SelfGrader achieves strong performance with low false positive rates, minimal memory overhead, and reduced latency, supporting its effectiveness in enhancing LLM safety.

Jailbreaking and Mitigation of Vulnerabilities in Large Language Models
Authors: Benji Peng, Hanxuan Chen, Keyu Chen, Qian Niu, Ziqian Bi, Ming Liu, Pohsun Feng, Tianyang Wang, Lawrence K. Q. Yan, Yizhu Wen, Yichao Zhang, Caitlyn Heqi Yin, Xinyuan Song, Riyang Bao, Jiacheng Shi
Venue: Eureka 1(1) (2026) 26-61
First: 2024-10-20T00:00:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-27T16:38:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed artificial intelligence by advancing natural language understanding and generation, enabling applications across fields beyond healthcare, software engineering, and conversational systems. Despite these advancements in the past few years, LLMs have shown considerable vulnerabilities, particularly to prompt injection and jailbreaking attacks. This review analyzes the state of research on these vulnerabilities and presents available defense strategies. We roughly categorize attack approaches into prompt-based, model-based, multimodal, and multilingual, covering techniques such as adversarial prompting, backdoor injections, and cross-modality exploits. We also review various defense mechanisms, including prompt filtering, transformation, alignment techniques, multi-agent defenses, and self-regulation, evaluating their strengths and shortcomings. We also discuss key metrics and benchmarks used to assess LLM safety and robustness, noting challenges like the quantification of attack success in interactive contexts and biases in existing datasets. Identifying current research gaps, we suggest future directions for resilient alignment strategies, advanced defenses against evolving attacks, automation of jailbreak detection, and consideration of ethical and societal impacts. This review emphasizes the need for continued research and cooperation within the AI community to enhance LLM security and ensure their safe deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型的越狱与漏洞缓解
大型语言模型（LLMs）通过推动自然语言理解和生成，改变了人工智能，使其在医疗、软件工程和对话系统等领域的应用得以实现。尽管近年来取得了这些进展，LLMs仍显示出相当大的脆弱性，特别是对提示注入和越狱攻击。本文回顾了这些漏洞的研究现状，并提出了可用的防御策略。我们大致将攻击方法分为基于提示、基于模型、多模态和多语言，涵盖对抗性提示、后门注入和跨模态利用等技术。我们还回顾了各种防御机制，包括提示过滤、转换、对齐技术、多智能体防御和自我调节，评估其优缺点。我们讨论了用于评估LLM安全性和鲁棒性的关键指标和基准，指出了在交互环境中量化攻击成功率和现有数据集中的偏见等挑战。识别当前研究空白，我们建议未来在弹性对齐策略、针对不断演变的攻击的高级防御、越狱检测的自动化以及伦理和社会影响的考虑等方面的研究方向。本文强调了在AI社区内持续研究和合作的必要性，以增强LLM安全性并确保其安全部署。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the significant vulnerabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) to various attacks, such as prompt injection and jailbreaking, which have emerged despite their advancements in natural language processing. Previous methods for defending against these vulnerabilities, including prompt filtering and transformation techniques, have shown limitations in effectiveness and adaptability. The proposed approach emphasizes a comprehensive review of existing attack strategies and defense mechanisms, identifying gaps in current research and suggesting future directions for improving LLM security. The methodology includes categorizing attack types and evaluating defense strategies, ultimately contributing to a deeper understanding of LLM vulnerabilities and the development of more robust safety measures. The findings highlight the need for ongoing research and collaboration to enhance LLM resilience, ensuring their safe application across diverse fields.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在面对各种攻击（如提示注入和越狱）时的显著脆弱性，尽管这些模型在自然语言处理方面取得了进展。以往的防御方法，如提示过滤和转换技术，在有效性和适应性方面存在局限。所提出的方法强调对现有攻击策略和防御机制的全面审查，识别当前研究中的空白，并建议未来改进LLM安全性的方向。该方法论包括对攻击类型的分类和对防御策略的评估，最终有助于更好地理解LLM的脆弱性并开发更强大的防御措施。本文强调了AI社区持续研究和合作的必要性，以增强LLM的安全性和可靠性，解决量化攻击成功率和数据集偏见等挑战，从而支持安全部署的目标。
Got a Secret? LLM Agents Can't Keep It: Evaluating Privacy in Multi-Agent Systems
Authors: Aman Priyanshu, Supriti Vijay, Esha Pahwa
First: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM safety evaluations predominantly test models in isolation, yet deployed AI agents increasingly operate within persistent social environments alongside other agents. We introduce a Moltbook-style simulation platform where thousands of LLM agents interact across communities over a simulated month, and use it to evaluate privacy as a downstream safety concern under varying degrees of social pressure. We find that shifting from single turn to multi turn social evaluation amplifies privacy violations (CIMemories 19.95% to Ours 45.30% across OpenAI models), that leakage is socially contagious, with agents 8 times more likely to disclose sensitive information after observing a peer do so, and that explicit privacy instructions reduce but do not eliminate this effect, leaving leakage rates above 37.8% even with safeguards. Our findings suggest that static chat based safety benchmarks systematically underestimate risks in agentic deployment, and that social context alone is sufficient to elicit sensitive disclosures that single turn evaluations would never surface.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有秘密吗？LLM代理无法保密：多代理系统中的隐私评估
LLM安全评估主要在孤立环境中测试模型，但部署的AI代理越来越多地在与其他代理的持久社交环境中操作。我们引入了一种Moltbook风格的模拟平台，在该平台上，数千个LLM代理在模拟的一个月内跨社区互动，并利用它评估在不同社交压力下的隐私作为下游安全问题。我们发现，从单轮到多轮社交评估的转变会加剧隐私侵犯（CIMemories 19.95%到我们的45.30%，在OpenAI模型中），泄露是社交传染的，代理在观察到同伴泄露后泄露敏感信息的可能性增加8倍，并且明确的隐私指令虽然减少但并未消除这一效应，即使有保护措施，泄露率仍高于37.8%。我们的发现表明，静态基于聊天的安全基准系统性低估了代理部署中的风险，仅社交背景就足以引发敏感信息的披露，而单轮评估永远无法揭示这些信息。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacy of current LLM safety evaluations, which typically assess models in isolation, failing to account for the social dynamics present in multi-agent systems. Previous methods have overlooked the impact of social interactions on privacy violations, leading to an underestimation of risks in real-world deployments. This paper proposes a Moltbook-style simulation platform that allows thousands of LLM agents to interact over a simulated month, effectively capturing the influence of social pressure on privacy breaches. The study reveals that transitioning from single-turn to multi-turn evaluations significantly increases privacy violations, with rates rising from 19.95% to 45.30% across OpenAI models, and highlights that agents are more likely to disclose sensitive information after witnessing peers do so. The findings indicate that existing static benchmarks are insufficient for evaluating safety in agentic contexts, emphasizing the need for dynamic assessments that consider social environments.

Evolving and Detecting Multi-Turn Deception using Geometric Signatures
Authors: Surender Suresh Kumar, Mary L. Cummings
First: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety defenses for large language models (LLMs) are typically trained and evaluated on single-turn prompts, yet real attacks often unfold as indirect, multi-turn probing. To defend against this more nuanced form of deception, we present a unified pipeline that generates realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets via multi-objective genetic prompt optimization with co-evolving mutation operators. We validate this dataset through a human study, which also revealed that early generations yielded the most convincing deception and practical constraints such as adherence filtering and ordering effects. Using this data, we were able to detect deceptive attempts to access prohibited information using simple, explainable geometric signals in embedding space coupled with a lightweight feed-forward classifier. Three geometric features (angular coverage, distance ratio, and linearity) augmented with pairwise similarity statistics led to a compact predictive model that achieved consistently high recall (0.89) across base, reworded, and truncated (three-turn) scenarios, with test-time F1 ranging from 0.74-0.86. The results support a central hypothesis that multi-turn deceptive intent leaves a stable geometric footprint that enables lightweight, transparent screening without expensive end-to-end training. We further discuss responsible uses, limitations, and paths toward larger, more diverse human-evaluated datasets. The primary contribution to artificial intelligence is the multi-objective evolutionary framework for prompt generation, and the engineering application is the deployment of a lightweight geometric detection system for LLM safety infrastructure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用几何特征演变和检测多轮欺骗
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全防御通常在单轮提示上进行训练和评估，但真实攻击往往以间接的多轮探测形式展开。为了防御这种更微妙的欺骗形式，我们提出了一个统一的流程，通过多目标遗传提示优化和共同演变的变异操作生成现实的多轮欺骗问题集。我们通过人类研究验证了该数据集，研究还揭示了早期生成的欺骗最具说服力，以及遵循过滤和排序效应等实际限制。利用这些数据，我们能够使用简单、可解释的几何信号在嵌入空间中检测试图访问禁止信息的欺骗行为，并结合轻量级前馈分类器。三个几何特征（角度覆盖、距离比和线性）与成对相似性统计相结合，形成了一个紧凑的预测模型，在基础、改写和截断（三轮）场景中实现了一致的高召回率（0.89），测试时F1值范围为0.74-0.86。结果支持一个中心假设，即多轮欺骗意图留下稳定的几何足迹，使得无需昂贵的端到端训练即可实现轻量、透明的筛选。我们进一步讨论了负责任的使用、局限性以及朝向更大、更具多样性的人类评估数据集的路径。对人工智能的主要贡献是用于提示生成的多目标进化框架，工程应用是为LLM安全基础设施部署轻量级几何检测系统。

This research addresses the inadequacy of existing safety defenses for large language models (LLMs), which are primarily evaluated on single-turn prompts, while real-world attacks often involve multi-turn interactions. Previous methods lack the capability to effectively handle this complexity, prompting the authors to propose a unified pipeline that utilizes multi-objective genetic prompt optimization to generate realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets. The study's contribution lies in the development of this evolutionary framework for prompt generation and a lightweight geometric detection system that identifies deceptive attempts using geometric signals in embedding space. The methodology involves generating deceptive prompts and employing a feed-forward classifier based on geometric features, achieving high recall rates (0.89) and F1 scores ranging from 0.74 to 0.86 across various scenarios, thereby supporting the hypothesis that multi-turn deception leaves a detectable geometric footprint, which facilitates efficient screening without extensive training.

$D^2$-Monitor: Dynamic Safety Monitoring for Diffusion LLMs via Hesitation-Aware Routing
Authors: Aoxi Liu, Yupeng Chen, James Oldfield, Guanzhe Hong, Junchi Yu, Baoyuan Wu, Philip Torr, Adel Bibi
First: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the emergence of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) as an alternative to autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs), safety monitoring for D-LLMs remains largely unexplored. Unlike AR-LLMs, D-LLMs generate text through a multi-step denoising process, exposing intermediate hidden representations that may contain safety-relevant information unavailable in standard single-step monitoring setups. Motivated by the suitability of lightweight probes for always-on monitoring, we analyze which trajectory-level signals best indicate when such probes are likely to struggle. We find that the most informative signal is safety hesitation: intermediate hidden states repeatedly falling within a small margin of the probe's decision boundary. The number of such hesitation steps in D-LLM's trajectory predicts probe failure effectively, providing a proxy of sample difficulty. Building on this analysis, we propose $D^2$-Monitor, a bi-level safety monitor for D-LLMs. $D^2$-Monitor adopts a lightweight probe as an always-on monitor to jointly estimate hesitation and perform base classification. When the hesitation level exceeds a threshold, a more expressive but computationally heavier probe is activated. This dynamic routing mechanism allocates monitoring resources efficiently at test time. Evaluated on 3 datasets (WildguardMix, ToxicChat, OpenAI-Moderation) across 4 D-LLMs, $D^2$-Monitor achieves state-of-the-art performance with a compact parameter footprint ($\leq$ 0.85M parameters), and exhibits the best trade-off between effectiveness and efficiency relative to 8 baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$D^2$-监控器：通过考虑犹豫的动态安全监控扩散大语言模型
尽管扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）作为自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）的替代方案已出现，但对D-LLMs的安全监控仍然基本未被探索。与AR-LLMs不同，D-LLMs通过多步骤去噪过程生成文本，暴露出可能包含安全相关信息的中间隐藏表示，而这些信息在标准单步监控设置中不可用。基于轻量级探针适合于始终在线监控的动机，我们分析了哪些轨迹级信号最能指示这些探针可能遇到困难。我们发现，最具信息量的信号是安全犹豫：中间隐藏状态反复落在探针决策边界的小范围内。D-LLM轨迹中此类犹豫步骤的数量有效预测探针失败，提供了样本难度的代理。基于此分析，我们提出了$D^2$-监控器，这是一个针对D-LLMs的双层安全监控器。$D^2$-监控器采用轻量级探针作为始终在线监控器，联合估计犹豫并进行基础分类。当犹豫水平超过阈值时，将激活一个更具表现力但计算负担更重的探针。该动态路由机制在测试时有效分配监控资源。在3个数据集（WildguardMix、ToxicChat、OpenAI-Moderation）上评估4个D-LLMs，$D^2$-监控器以紧凑的参数占用（≤ 0.85M参数）实现了最先进的性能，并在相对于8个基线之间展现了最佳的有效性与效率的权衡。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the gap in safety monitoring for diffusion large language models (D-LLMs), which have not been thoroughly explored compared to autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs). Previous methods primarily focused on single-step monitoring, which fails to utilize the intermediate hidden representations of D-LLMs that can provide crucial safety-related insights. The proposed approach, $D^2$-Monitor, introduces a bi-level safety monitoring system that leverages lightweight probes for continuous monitoring and activates a more complex probe when safety hesitation is detected, thus effectively addressing the limitations of existing methods. This method is well-motivated as it enhances the monitoring process by dynamically allocating resources based on the model's performance. The contribution of the paper lies in achieving state-of-the-art performance on three datasets (WildguardMix, ToxicChat, OpenAI-Moderation) with a compact parameter size of less than 0.85 million parameters, demonstrating an optimal balance between effectiveness and efficiency compared to eight baseline methods.
本研究针对扩散大型语言模型（D-LLMs）在安全监控方面的不足进行探讨，而这一领域相较于自回归大型语言模型（AR-LLMs）尚未得到充分研究。以往的方法主要集中在单步监控，未能利用D-LLMs的多步去噪过程，这一过程揭示了包含安全相关信息的中间隐藏表示。所提出的方法$D^2$-Monitor引入了一种双层安全监控系统，利用轻量级探针进行持续监控，并在检测到安全犹豫时激活更复杂的探针，从而有效分配资源。该方法的提出是基于对D-LLMs中有效安全措施需求的合理动机。论文的贡献在于其创新的动态路由机制，经过在三个数据集上的评估，展示了以低于85万参数的紧凑参数足迹实现的最先进性能，并在与八个基线方法的比较中达到了有效性与效率的最佳平衡。
Reflect-Guard: Enhancing LLM Safeguards against Adversarial Prompts via Logical Self-Reflection
Authors: Lixing Lin, Juli You, Yue Li, Luyun Lin, Yiqing Wang, Zhen Zhang, Moxuan Zheng
First: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 2 figures, and 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) safety classifiers such as Llama Guard are effective at detecting overtly harmful prompts but remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that disguise malicious intent through role-play scenarios, fictional framing, and indirect requests. We present Reflect-Guard, a method that augments LLM-based safety classifiers with chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning. Our approach distills analytical reasoning from GPT-4o-mini into structured reflection annotations, then trains Llama-Guard-3-8B via QLoRA to generate logical self-reflections before issuing safety verdicts. Using only 1000 training examples and updating just 0.5% of model parameters (~42M), Reflect-Guard achieves substantial improvements on two challenging benchmarks. On WildGuardTest, F1 score improves from 0.770 to 0.842 (+7.2 pp), with recall on adversarial prompts increasing from 0.513 to 0.921 (+40.8 pp). On JailbreakBench, the attack success rate drops from 10.3% to 1.8%, representing an 82.5% relative reduction. These gains are especially pronounced on adversarial inputs, where the explicit reasoning step enables the model to see through obfuscation techniques that defeat standard pattern-matching approaches. Our results demonstrate that teaching safety classifiers to reason about adversarial intent, rather than simply classify surface patterns, is a promising direction for robust LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Reflect-Guard：通过逻辑自我反思增强大型语言模型对抗性提示的安全防护
大型语言模型（LLM）安全分类器如Llama Guard在检测明显有害提示方面有效，但仍然容易受到通过角色扮演场景、虚构框架和间接请求伪装恶意意图的对抗性越狱攻击的影响。我们提出了Reflect-Guard，这是一种通过参数高效微调增强LLM基础安全分类器的链式思维自我反思能力的方法。我们的方法将GPT-4o-mini的分析推理提炼为结构化反思注释，然后通过QLoRA训练Llama-Guard-3-8B，以在发出安全裁决之前生成逻辑自我反思。仅使用1000个训练示例并更新0.5%的模型参数（约4200万），Reflect-Guard在两个具有挑战性的基准测试中取得了显著改善。在WildGuardTest中，F1分数从0.770提高到0.842（+7.2个百分点），对抗性提示的召回率从0.513提高到0.921（+40.8个百分点）。在JailbreakBench中，攻击成功率从10.3%降至1.8%，相对减少82.5%。这些提升在对抗性输入上尤为明显，明确的推理步骤使模型能够看穿击败标准模式匹配方法的混淆技术。我们的结果表明，教导安全分类器推理对抗性意图，而不仅仅是分类表面模式，是增强LLM安全性的一个有前景的方向。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of existing large language model (LLM) safety classifiers, which are effective at identifying overtly harmful prompts but are susceptible to adversarial attacks that mask malicious intent. Previous methods primarily relied on pattern matching, which can be circumvented by sophisticated obfuscation techniques. The proposed Reflect-Guard method enhances LLM safety classifiers by incorporating chain-of-thought self-reflection through parameter-efficient fine-tuning, allowing the model to generate logical self-reflections before making safety judgments. This approach is well-motivated as it teaches classifiers to reason about adversarial intent rather than merely classify prompts based on surface patterns. The methodology involves distilling reasoning from GPT-4o-mini and training Llama-Guard-3-8B with only 1000 examples, resulting in significant performance improvements on two benchmarks: an F1 score increase from 0.770 to 0.842 on WildGuardTest and a reduction in attack success rate from 10.3% to 1.8% on JailbreakBench, demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed method in enhancing LLM safety against adversarial prompts.
本研究解决了现有大型语言模型（LLM）安全分类器（如Llama Guard）的局限性，这些分类器能够有效检测有害提示，但容易受到伪装恶意意图的对抗性越狱攻击。以往的方法主要依赖于模式匹配，这在面对复杂的模糊技术时效果不佳。提出的Reflect-Guard通过引入链式思维自我反思，增强了安全分类器的能力，采用参数高效的微调方法，使模型能够推理对抗性意图。这种方法是合理的，因为它将重点从简单分类转向分析推理。该方法论涉及将GPT-4o-mini的推理提炼为结构化注释，并使用QLoRA对Llama-Guard-3-8B进行训练，仅使用1000个示例和最小的参数更新。结果显示显著的性能提升，WildGuardTest上的F1分数从0.770提高到0.842，而JailbreakBench上的攻击成功率从10.3%降至1.8%，证明了该方法在增强LLM对抗性提示安全性方面的有效性。
RouteScan: A Non-Intrusive Approach to Auditing MoE LLMs Safety via Expert Routing Telemetry
Authors: Bo Lv, Zhiheng Xu, KeDong Xiu, Ruyi Ding, Tianhang Zheng, Zhibo Wang, Kui Ren
First: 2026-05-24T02:06:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:06:44+00:00
Comments: 20 pages. Under submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures have become an increasingly important paradigm for scaling Large Language Models (LLMs). As MoE models are increasingly deployed in real-world services, safety auditing becomes necessary to verify whether these models produce or facilitate harmful behaviors during operation. However, existing content-based auditing methods typically require access to user prompts, model inputs, or generated outputs, potentially exposing sensitive user information and creating a fundamental tension between LLM safety and user privacy. On the other hand, we observe that, in MoE models, sparse expert routing maps different inputs to activate different expert-execution patterns, producing measurable footprints in low-level GPU execution telemetry. Inspired by this observation, we propose RouteScan, a non-intrusive auditing framework for detecting harmful behaviors through GPU-level expert routing telemetry. Specifically, RouteScan utilizes the number of active GPU threads allocated to expert modules during the prefilling phase as a discriminative micro-architectural fingerprint, and builds a lightweight detection pipeline that isolates cross-domain invariant risk indicators for the precise identification of malicious prompts. Comprehensive evaluations on open-source MoE LLMs with distinct routing designs demonstrate that RouteScan achieves strong generalization, with an AUROC exceeding 0.93 on unseen harmful domains and 0.96 under novel jailbreak wrappers. Moreover, empirical inversion tests show that the collected expert routing telemetry provides limited information for prompt reconstruction, suggesting a practical privacy advantage over content-based auditing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RouteScan：通过专家路由遥测对MoE LLM安全性进行非侵入式审计的方法
混合专家（MoE）架构已成为扩展大型语言模型（LLM）的一个越来越重要的范式。随着MoE模型在现实服务中的日益部署，安全审计变得必要，以验证这些模型在操作过程中是否产生或促进有害行为。然而，现有的基于内容的审计方法通常需要访问用户提示、模型输入或生成的输出，这可能暴露敏感用户信息，并在LLM安全性与用户隐私之间产生根本性矛盾。另一方面，我们观察到，在MoE模型中，稀疏专家路由将不同输入映射到激活不同的专家执行模式，产生可测量的低级GPU执行遥测足迹。受此观察启发，我们提出了RouteScan，一个通过GPU级专家路由遥测检测有害行为的非侵入式审计框架。具体而言，RouteScan利用在预填充阶段分配给专家模块的活跃GPU线程数量作为区分性微架构指纹，并构建一个轻量级检测管道，隔离跨域不变风险指标，以精确识别恶意提示。对具有不同路由设计的开源MoE LLM的全面评估表明，RouteScan实现了强大的泛化能力，在未见有害领域的AUROC超过0.93，在新型越狱包装下达到0.96。此外，经验反演测试表明，收集的专家路由遥测提供的提示重建信息有限，表明相较于基于内容的审计方法具有实际的隐私优势。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing need for safety auditing in Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures used in Large Language Models (LLMs), which are increasingly deployed in real-world applications. Traditional content-based auditing methods pose privacy risks by requiring access to sensitive user data, creating a conflict between ensuring model safety and protecting user privacy. The proposed approach, RouteScan, differs by leveraging GPU-level expert routing telemetry, which captures the execution patterns of different experts without exposing user prompts or outputs. This method is well-motivated as it provides a non-intrusive means of detecting harmful behaviors while maintaining user confidentiality. The contribution of the paper lies in establishing a lightweight detection pipeline that utilizes active GPU thread counts as a micro-architectural fingerprint to identify malicious prompts. Evaluations on open-source MoE LLMs show that RouteScan achieves an AUROC of over 0.93 on unseen harmful domains and 0.96 with novel jailbreak wrappers, indicating strong performance and supporting its goal of safe auditing without compromising privacy.
本研究解决了在大型语言模型（LLM）中使用的专家混合（MoE）架构中日益增长的安全审计需求，因为现有的基于内容的方法通过要求访问敏感信息而对用户隐私构成风险。传统的审计技术往往妨碍用户机密性，而提出的RouteScan框架利用GPU级专家路由遥测来检测有害行为，而不暴露用户提示或输出。该方法的动机在于观察到不同输入激活不同的专家执行模式，这些模式可以作为GPU遥测中的可测量足迹进行捕获。RouteScan引入了一种轻量级检测管道，通过分析模型预填充阶段分配的活动GPU线程数量来识别恶意提示。对各种开源MoE LLM的实验结果表明，RouteScan在未见有害领域的AUROC超过0.93，表明其在确保安全性同时维护用户隐私方面的有效性。
BarrierSteer: LLM Safety via Learning Barrier Steering
Authors: Thanh Q. Tran, Arun Verma, Kiwan Wong, Bryan Kian Hsiang Low, Daniela Rus, Wei Xiao
First: 2026-02-23T18:19:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-21T18:01:19+00:00
Comments: This paper introduces SafeBarrier, a framework that enforces safety in large language models by steering their latent representations with control barrier functions during inference, reducing adversarial and unsafe outputs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Despite the strong performance of large language models (LLMs) across diverse tasks, their susceptibility to adversarial attacks and unsafe content generation remains a significant obstacle to deployment, particularly in high-stakes settings. Addressing this challenge requires safety mechanisms that are both practically effective and theoretically grounded. In this paper, we introduce BarrierSteer, a novel inference-time framework that improves response safety by embedding learned nonlinear safety constraints directly into the model's latent representation space. BarrierSteer treats hidden-state safety classifiers as Control Barrier Functions (CBFs), enabling constraint-guided steering of unsafe latent trajectories during generation. By composing multiple safety constraints through efficient constraint merging without modifying the underlying LLM parameters, BarrierSteer preserves model utility. We provide theoretical results showing that applying CBFs in the latent space yields a principled, modular, and computationally efficient approach for steering with respect to learned safety constraints, with guarantees conditional on the learned barriers capturing the intended safety property. Our extensive experimental results across multiple model families and datasets demonstrate that BarrierSteer substantially reduces adversarial attack success rates and unsafe generations, outperforming the existing method. The code is available in our \href{https://github.com/thanhquangtran/BarrierSteer}{GitHub repository}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BarrierSteer：通过学习障碍引导实现LLM安全
尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种任务中表现出色，但它们对对抗性攻击和不安全内容生成的易感性仍然是部署中的重大障碍，特别是在高风险环境中。解决这一挑战需要既有效又有理论基础的安全机制。本文介绍了BarrierSteer，这是一种新颖的推理时框架，通过将学习到的非线性安全约束直接嵌入模型的潜在表示空间来提高响应安全性。BarrierSteer将隐藏状态安全分类器视为控制障碍函数（CBFs），使得在生成过程中能够对不安全的潜在轨迹进行约束引导。通过高效的约束合并组合多个安全约束，而不修改底层LLM参数，BarrierSteer保持了模型的实用性。我们提供了理论结果，表明在潜在空间中应用CBFs提供了一种原则性、模块化和计算高效的引导方法，能够根据学习到的障碍捕捉预期的安全属性。我们在多个模型系列和数据集上的广泛实验结果表明，BarrierSteer显著降低了对抗性攻击成功率和不安全生成，超越了现有方法。代码可在我们的\href{https://github.com/thanhquangtran/BarrierSteer}{GitHub仓库}中获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the significant challenge of ensuring safety in large language models (LLMs), which are prone to adversarial attacks and unsafe content generation, particularly in high-stakes applications. Previous methods have struggled with effectively integrating safety mechanisms without compromising model performance. The proposed approach, BarrierSteer, introduces a novel framework that embeds learned nonlinear safety constraints into the model's latent representation space, utilizing Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) to guide the generation process while maintaining the utility of the LLM. This method is well-motivated by the need for a theoretically grounded and practically effective solution to enhance response safety. The paper contributes a principled and computationally efficient strategy for steering LLMs with respect to safety constraints, demonstrating through extensive experiments that BarrierSteer significantly reduces adversarial attack success rates and unsafe outputs compared to existing methods, thus supporting its goals of improving LLM safety.

Revisiting Robustness for LLM Safety Alignment via Selective Geometry Control
Authors: Yonghui Yang, Wenjian Tao, Jilong Liu, Xingyu Zhu, Junfeng Fang, Weibiao Huang, Le Wu, Richang Hong, Tat-Sent Chua
First: 2026-02-07T03:46:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-21T07:39:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Safety alignment of large language models remains brittle under domain shift and noisy preference supervision. Most existing robust alignment methods focus on uncertainty in alignment data, while overlooking optimization-induced fragility in preference-based objectives. In this work, we revisit robustness for LLM safety alignment from an optimization geometry perspective, and argue that robustness failures cannot be addressed by data-centric methods alone. We propose \textit{ShaPO}, a geometry-aware preference optimization framework that enforces worst-case alignment objectives via selective geometry control over alignment-critical parameter subspace. By avoiding uniform geometry constraints, ShaPO mitigates the over-regularization that can harm robustness under distribution shift. We instantiate ShaPO at two levels: token-level ShaPO stabilizes likelihood-based surrogate optimization, while reward-level ShaPO enforces reward-consistent optimization under noisy supervision. Across diverse safety benchmarks and noisy preference settings, ShaPO consistently improves safety robustness over popular preference optimization methods. Moreover, ShaPO composes cleanly with data-robust objectives, yielding additional gains and empirically supporting the proposed optimization-geometry perspective. The code is available at https://github.com/liujilong0116/ShaPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过选择性几何控制重新审视大型语言模型的安全对齐鲁棒性
大型语言模型的安全对齐在领域转移和噪声偏好监督下仍然脆弱。现有的大多数鲁棒对齐方法关注对齐数据的不确定性，而忽视了基于偏好的目标中优化引起的脆弱性。在本研究中，我们从优化几何的角度重新审视LLM安全对齐的鲁棒性，并认为鲁棒性失败不能仅通过以数据为中心的方法来解决。我们提出了\textit{ShaPO}，一个几何感知的偏好优化框架，通过对对齐关键参数子空间的选择性几何控制来强制执行最坏情况对齐目标。通过避免均匀几何约束，ShaPO减轻了在分布转移下可能损害鲁棒性的过度正则化。我们在两个层面上实例化ShaPO：令牌级ShaPO稳定基于似然的替代优化，而奖励级ShaPO在噪声监督下强制执行奖励一致的优化。在多样的安全基准和噪声偏好设置中，ShaPO始终优于流行的偏好优化方法，提高了安全鲁棒性。此外，ShaPO与数据鲁棒目标良好组合，带来额外收益，并在经验上支持所提出的优化几何视角。代码可在https://github.com/liujilong0116/ShaPO获取。

This method is well-motivated as it seeks to enhance safety alignment through a novel optimization geometry perspective. The paper demonstrates that ShaPO significantly improves safety robustness across various benchmarks and noisy preference scenarios compared to existing preference optimization techniques, while also integrating effectively with data-robust objectives to achieve further performance enhancements.

On-Policy Consistency Training Improves LLM Safety with Minimal Capability Degradation
Authors: Andy Han, Kristina Fujimoto, Avidan Shah, Kiet Nguyen, Kai Xu, Chen Yueh-Han, Ilia Sucholutsky, Rico Angell
First: 2026-05-20T23:56:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-20T23:56:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligned models can misbehave in several ways: they are often sycophantic, fall victim to jailbreaks, or fail to include appropriate safety warnings. Consistency training is a promising new alignment paradigm to mitigate such failures by training invariants into the model using contrastive input pairs. Existing consistency training procedures generate the supervision signal once, offline, and use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to update the model. Unfortunately, the resulting models tend to merely memorize the surface forms of the training distribution and thus generalize poorly and regress in their capabilities. We introduce On-Policy Consistency Training (OPCT), a new consistency training approach where the objective is computed over the model's own responses to prompts, supervised by itself conditioned on corresponding contrastive prompts. We evaluate OPCT on three safety axes: sycophancy, jailbreaking, and safety awareness. Across three model families, OPCT outperforms its SFT counterpart on all safety desiderata. It nearly halves the sycophancy rate relative to baseline (8.1% vs. 15.4%, compared to 11.2% for SFT). Under an adaptive per-target attacker, OPCT holds jailbreak defense success near 99% on held-out jailbreak behaviors, whereas SFT achieves 87% on average. On safety awareness, OPCT outperforms SFT in two out of three models, and matches it on the other. OPCT also largely avoids the capability regressions that SFT induces, such as a 28-point drop on MATH-500. Our results suggest that consistency training is best implemented as OPCT rather than as SFT, especially when generalization beyond the training distribution is desired.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于策略的一致性训练通过最小能力退化提高大型语言模型的安全性
对齐模型可能以多种方式表现不当：它们往往表现得过于谄媚，容易受到越狱攻击，或未能包含适当的安全警告。一致性训练是一种有前景的新对齐范式，通过使用对比输入对将不变性训练到模型中，以减轻这些失败。现有的一致性训练程序仅在离线状态下生成一次监督信号，并使用监督微调（SFT）来更新模型。不幸的是，结果模型往往仅仅记住训练分布的表面形式，因此泛化能力差，能力退化。我们引入了基于策略的一致性训练（OPCT），这是一种新的一致性训练方法，其目标是基于模型对提示的自身响应进行计算，由相应的对比提示进行自我监督。我们在三个安全维度上评估OPCT：谄媚、越狱和安全意识。在三种模型系列中，OPCT在所有安全要求上均优于其SFT对应物。与基线相比，谄媚率几乎减半（8.1%对15.4%，而SFT为11.2%）。在自适应每个目标攻击者下，OPCT在保留的越狱行为上保持近99%的越狱防御成功率，而SFT平均为87%。在安全意识方面，OPCT在三种模型中的两种上优于SFT，另一种则持平。OPCT还在很大程度上避免了SFT引起的能力退化，例如在MATH-500上下降28分。我们的结果表明，一致性训练最好以OPCT的形式实施，而不是SFT，特别是在希望超越训练分布进行泛化时。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of aligned models, which often exhibit undesirable behaviors such as sycophancy and vulnerability to jailbreaks. Traditional consistency training methods generate supervision signals offline and rely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT), leading to poor generalization and capability regressions. The proposed On-Policy Consistency Training (OPCT) method computes objectives based on the model's own responses to prompts, enhancing self-supervision and mitigating the issues seen in SFT. The paper contributes by demonstrating that OPCT significantly improves safety metrics across three model families, achieving a nearly halved sycophancy rate and maintaining a high success rate against jailbreak attempts, while largely avoiding capability regressions. The methodology shows that OPCT is more effective than SFT in promoting model safety without sacrificing performance, particularly in tasks requiring generalization beyond the training distribution.
本研究解决了对齐模型常常表现出不良行为（如谄媚和易受越狱攻击）的问题，这可能会影响安全性。以往的方法依赖于离线监督微调（SFT）进行一致性训练，导致泛化能力差和能力回退。提出的在线一致性训练（OPCT）通过基于模型对提示的自身响应计算目标，从而增强自我监督，提高安全性而不降低能力。本文的贡献在于证明OPCT显著降低了谄媚率，几乎实现了对越狱攻击的完美防御，并在多个模型系列中保持安全意识，同时避免了与SFT相关的能力回退。该方法论通过在安全指标上评估OPCT，显示其在关键领域优于SFT，并有效支持提高模型安全性的目标。
CR4T: Rewrite-Based Guardrails for Adolescent LLM Safety
Authors: Heajun An, Qi Zhang, Vedanth Achanta, Jin-Hee Cho
First: 2026-05-20T18:16:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-20T18:16:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly embedded in adolescent digital environments, mediating information seeking, advice, and emotionally sensitive interactions. Yet existing safety mechanisms remain largely grounded in adult-centric norms and operationalize safety through refusal-oriented suppression. While such approaches may reduce immediate policy violations, they can also create conversational dead-ends, limit constructive guidance, and fail to address the developmental vulnerabilities inherent in adolescent-AI interactions. We argue that adolescent LLM safety should be framed not solely as a filtering problem, but as a socio-technical, developmentally aligned transformation problem. To operationalize this perspective, we propose Critique-and-Revise-for-Teenagers (CR4T), a model-agnostic safeguarding framework that selectively reconstructs unsafe or refusal-style outputs into ageappropriate, guidance-oriented responses while preserving benign intent. CR4T combines lightweight risk detection with domain-conditioned rewriting to remove risk-amplifying content, reduce unnecessary conversational shutdown, and introduce developmentally appropriate guidance. Experimental results show that targeted rewriting substantially reduces unsafe and refusal-oriented outcomes while avoiding unnecessary intervention on acceptable interactions. These findings suggest that selective response reconstruction offers a more human-centered alternative to refusal-centric guardrails for adolescent-facing LLM systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CR4T：基于重写的青少年大型语言模型安全防护
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地嵌入青少年的数字环境中，调解信息搜索、建议和情感敏感的互动。然而，现有的安全机制仍然主要基于成人中心的规范，并通过拒绝导向的压制来实现安全。虽然这种方法可能减少即时的政策违规，但也可能造成对话死胡同，限制建设性指导，并未能解决青少年与人工智能互动中固有的发展脆弱性。我们认为，青少年LLM安全不应仅仅被视为过滤问题，而应被框定为一个社会技术、发展对齐的转型问题。为了实现这一视角，我们提出了针对青少年的批评与修订（CR4T），这是一个模型无关的安全框架，选择性地将不安全或拒绝风格的输出重构为适龄的、指导导向的响应，同时保持良好的意图。CR4T结合轻量级风险检测与领域条件重写，以去除风险放大内容，减少不必要的对话中断，并引入发展适宜的指导。实验结果表明，针对性重写显著减少了不安全和拒绝导向的结果，同时避免了对可接受互动的不必要干预。这些发现表明，选择性响应重构为面向青少年的LLM系统提供了一种更以人为本的替代方案，取代了以拒绝为中心的防护措施。

Previous methods tend to create conversational dead-ends and fail to cater to the developmental needs of adolescents. The proposed approach, Critique-and-Revise-for-Teenagers (CR4T), shifts the focus from merely filtering content to a socio-technical transformation that reconstructs unsafe outputs into age-appropriate, guidance-oriented responses. This model-agnostic framework employs risk detection and domain-conditioned rewriting to mitigate risks while promoting constructive interactions. Experimental results indicate that CR4T significantly decreases unsafe and refusal-oriented outputs without hindering acceptable conversations, thus providing a more human-centered alternative for adolescent LLM safety.

Adaptive Probe-based Steering for Robust LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Junxi Chen, Junhao Dong, Xiaohua Xie
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-19T06:11:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-19T06:11:04+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 13 figures, accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent work has demonstrated the potential of contrastive steering for jailbreaking Large Language Models (LLMs). However, existing methods rely on limited and inherently biased contrastive prompts and require laborious manual tuning of steering strength, limiting their robustness and effectiveness. In this paper, we leverage the idea of model extraction to guide the learned steering vectors to approximate the ideal one and propose tuning the steering strength adaptively based on contrastive activations' statistics. Experiments demonstrate that our method notably improves the effectiveness and robustness of probe-based steering, without any extra contrastive prompts or laborious manual tuning. Being an attack paper, this paper focuses on revealing the breakdown of fortified LLMs, raising the average harmfulness score from 6\% to 70\%. Our code is available at https://github.com/fhdnskfbeuv/adaptiveSteering.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自适应探针的鲁棒LLM越狱引导
最近的研究展示了对比引导在越狱大型语言模型（LLMs）中的潜力。然而，现有方法依赖于有限且固有偏见的对比提示，并需要繁琐的手动调节引导强度，限制了其鲁棒性和有效性。本文利用模型提取的思想，引导学习到的引导向量逼近理想向量，并提出基于对比激活统计自适应调节引导强度。实验表明，我们的方法显著提高了基于探针的引导的有效性和鲁棒性，无需额外的对比提示或繁琐的手动调节。作为一篇攻击论文，本文重点揭示了强化LLMs的崩溃，将平均危害评分从6\%提高到70\%。我们的代码可在https://github.com/fhdnskfbeuv/adaptiveSteering获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of existing contrastive steering methods for jailbreaking Large Language Models (LLMs), which rely on biased prompts and require extensive manual tuning, thus compromising their robustness. The proposed approach introduces adaptive tuning of steering strength based on the statistical analysis of contrastive activations, improving upon previous methods by eliminating the need for additional prompts and reducing manual effort. This paper contributes to the field by enhancing the effectiveness and robustness of probe-based steering techniques, achieving a significant increase in harmfulness scores from 6% to 70% in experiments, thereby supporting its goal of revealing vulnerabilities in fortified LLMs. The methodology involves leveraging model extraction to guide steering vectors towards an ideal configuration, demonstrating a marked improvement in performance on the jailbreaking task.
本研究解决了现有对比引导方法在破解大型语言模型（LLMs）时的局限性，这些方法通常依赖于偏见提示并需要大量手动调节，从而降低了其鲁棒性。所提出的方法基于对比激活的统计数据自适应调节引导强度，改进了以往的方法，消除了对额外提示和手动调整的需求。本文通过显著增强探针引导技术的有效性和鲁棒性，为该领域做出了贡献。该方法论涉及利用模型提取引导引导向量朝理想配置发展，实验结果显示平均有害性评分从6%显著提高至70%，从而支持揭示强化LLMs脆弱性的目标。
LLM-Safety Evaluations Lack Robustness
Authors: Tim Beyer, Sophie Xhonneux, Simon Geisler, Gauthier Gidel, Leo Schwinn, Stephan Günnemann
First: 2025-03-04T12:55:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T17:54:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we argue that current safety alignment research efforts for large language models are hindered by many intertwined sources of noise, such as small datasets, methodological inconsistencies, and unreliable evaluation setups. This can, at times, make it impossible to evaluate and compare attacks and defenses fairly, thereby slowing progress. We systematically analyze the LLM safety evaluation pipeline, covering dataset curation, optimization strategies for automated red-teaming, response generation, and response evaluation using LLM judges. At each stage, we identify key issues and highlight their practical impact. We also propose a set of guidelines for reducing noise and bias in evaluations of future attack and defense papers. Lastly, we offer an opposing perspective, highlighting practical reasons for existing limitations. We believe that addressing the outlined problems in future research will improve the field's ability to generate easily comparable results and make measurable progress.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型安全评估缺乏稳健性
在本文中，我们认为当前针对大型语言模型的安全对齐研究受到许多交织的噪声源的阻碍，例如小数据集、方法不一致和不可靠的评估设置。这有时使得公平评估和比较攻击与防御变得不可能，从而减缓进展。我们系统分析了LLM安全评估流程，涵盖数据集策划、自动红队的优化策略、响应生成和使用LLM评审的响应评估。在每个阶段，我们识别关键问题并强调其实际影响。我们还提出了一套减少未来攻击和防御论文评估中的噪声和偏见的指导方针。最后，我们提供了一个对立的观点，强调现有局限性的实际原因。我们相信，解决未来研究中概述的问题将提高该领域生成易于比较结果和实现可测量进展的能力。

Babel: Jailbreaking Safety Attention via Obfuscation Distribution Optimized Sampling
Authors: Ziwei Wang, Jing Chen, Ruichao Liang, Zhi Wang, Yebo Feng, Ju Jia, Ruiying Du, Cong Wu, Yang Liu
First: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite rigorous safety alignment, Large Language Models (LLMs) remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing black-box methods often rely on heuristic templates or exhaustive trials, lacking mechanistic interpretability and query efficiency. In this study, we investigate an intrinsic vulnerability in the safety mechanisms of LLMs, where safety alignment relies on a small set of sparsely distributed attention heads, leaving much of the representational space weakly monitored. We formalize this phenomenon with a mathematical jailbreaking model that characterizes the delicate boundary of effective text obfuscation and analytically explains observed jailbreak behaviors. Guided by this model, we propose Babel, an efficient black-box attack framework that exploits the identified safety gap through systematic obfuscation sampling with iterative, feedback-driven distribution refinement, enabling reliable and high-success jailbreak attacks without access to model internals. Comprehensive evaluations on frontier commercial models demonstrate that Babel achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates and superior query efficiency. Specifically, compared to state-of-the-art methods, Babel increases the attack success rate on GPT-4o from 41.33% to 82.67% and on Claude-3-5-haiku from 38.33% to 78.33% within an average of 40 queries, providing a robust red-teaming methodology for LLMs safety research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巴别：通过模糊分布优化采样破解安全注意力
尽管进行了严格的安全对齐，大型语言模型（LLMs）仍然容易受到越狱攻击。现有的黑箱方法通常依赖于启发式模板或穷举试验，缺乏机制可解释性和查询效率。在本研究中，我们调查了LLMs安全机制中的内在脆弱性，其中安全对齐依赖于一小组稀疏分布的注意力头，导致大部分表示空间监控不足。我们用数学越狱模型形式化这一现象，描述有效文本模糊化的微妙边界，并分析观察到的越狱行为。在该模型的指导下，我们提出了Babel，一个高效的黑箱攻击框架，通过系统的模糊采样和迭代反馈驱动的分布优化，利用识别出的安全漏洞，实现可靠且高成功率的越狱攻击，而无需访问模型内部。对前沿商业模型的全面评估表明，Babel实现了最先进的攻击成功率和优越的查询效率。具体而言，与最先进的方法相比，Babel将GPT-4o的攻击成功率从41.33%提高到82.67%，将Claude-3-5-haiku的攻击成功率从38.33%提高到78.33%，平均在40个查询内，提供了一种强大的红队方法论用于LLMs安全研究。

The methodology demonstrates significant improvements in attack success rates, achieving 82.67% on GPT-4o and 78.33% on Claude-3-5-haiku within an average of 40 queries, thereby providing a robust framework for LLM safety research.

IndicSafe: A Benchmark for Evaluating Multilingual LLM Safety in South Asia
Authors: Priyaranjan Pattnayak, Sanchari Chowdhuri
First: 2026-03-18T16:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T17:06:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) are deployed in multilingual settings, their safety behavior in culturally diverse, low-resource languages remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic evaluation of LLM safety across 12 Indic languages, spoken by over 1.2 billion people but underrepresented in LLM training data. Using a dataset of 6,000 culturally grounded prompts spanning caste, religion, gender, health, and politics, we assess 10 leading LLMs on translated variants of the prompt. Our analysis reveals significant safety drift: cross-language agreement is just 12.8\%, and \texttt{SAFE} rate variance exceeds 17\% across languages. Some models over-refuse benign prompts in low-resource scripts, overflag politically sensitive topics, while others fail to flag unsafe generations. We quantify these failures using prompt-level entropy, category bias scores, and multilingual consistency indices. Our findings highlight critical safety generalization gaps in multilingual LLMs and show that safety alignment does not transfer evenly across languages. We release \textsc{IndicSafe}, the first benchmark to enable culturally informed safety evaluation for Indic deployments, and advocate for language-aware alignment strategies grounded in regional harms.
中文标题/摘要
